 vahiin survey main 5 fisadi log is vishay par koi raay nahin rakhte hai

 aankadon ke mutabik is samay tak jahaan 48 fisadi log maanate the ki bhrashtachar kaa str modi sarkaar ke kaarykaal se pehle ke str se bad gaya he vahiin 28 fisadi logon ko modi sarkaar or purv kii manmohan sarkaar ke kaarykaal main vyaapt bhrashtachar ke str main koi antar nahin dikhaai diya

 is samay tak 23 fisadi logon ko lagata tha ki modi sarkaar ne safaltaapurvak bhrashtachar par lagaam lagane kaa kaam kiya he

 com / y4oazapqxo a city of Uttar Pradesh, the country's largest state, is again facing the brunt of mob violence
 somvaar ko pashchimi uttar pradesh ke bulandshahr main jo hua wo daraane vaala tha
 The angry mob became so uncontrollable that it killed a policeman
 gokshi ke shaq main hue is bavaal main syana thane ke police inspector subodh kumaar ne apni jaan ganvaai
 Sub Inspector Suresh Kumar, who was present on the spot, told about how this accident happened and how the situation went on deteriorating
 ajtak se baat karte hue suresh kumaar ne kaha ki achaanak 500-600 logon kii bheed ai or usne police chaowkee par hamalaa kar diya
 Meanwhile, Police Inspector Subodh Kumar was also targeted
 suresh ne bataaya ki bheed ne is dauraan patharbaji shuru kar di, unhen bhi pathar laga
 Because of which they also fell there
 unhone bataaya jo bheed ai unke paas pathar, lathi-danda sabhi kuch tha, haalanki unhone kisi ke paas koi hathiyaar nahin dekha tha
 Suresh Kumar said that Inspector Subodh Kumar's life could have been saved, but it was not due to the crowd
 unhone bataaya ki jis dauraan subodh kumaar ghayal hue, agar tabhi unhen ilaaj ke liye aspataal le jaaya jaataa to shaayad unki jaan naa jaati
 The crowd did not allow him to be taken to the hospital
 kya hua bulandshahr main
 
 
 Significantly, on Monday (december 3), a furore started in Kobulandshahr's Siana police station area after fear of cow slaughter
 jisaki shikaayat milane par subodh kumaar polisbal ke saath maukey par pahunche the
 An FIR was being registered in this case, at the same time, a crowd of about 400 people from three villages filled the remains of the alleged cow dynasty in the tractor-trolley and reached the Chingrawathi police outpost and blocked it
 isi dauraan bheed jab ugr hui to police ne kaabo paane ke liye lathicharge or aansu gas ke gole chode or jald hi vahaan firing bhi hone lagi
 In which Subodh Kumar was injured and a young man was also injured
 subodh kumaar ko aspataal le jane se roka gaya or unki car par jamkar patharav bhi kiya gaya
 It has now been confirmed that Subodh Kumar died of a bullet
 aapako bataa den ki bulandshahr ke jiladhikari ke anusaar,subodh kumaarake sir main goli lagi thi, jis kaaran unki maut hui he
 He has also told that after the attack, when Subodh Kumar tried to save himself by going towards the farm, the mob attacked him there too
 chauthe charan ke matdaan ke dauraan kai jagahon se iviem kharaab hone kii shikaayatein aa rahi hai
 Voting has not started due to EVM malfunctions at several booths in Uttar Pradesh, Bihar, Jharkhand and West Bengal
 iske kaaran vot daalane pahunche matadaata hangaamaa kar rahe hai

 jharkhand ke palamu seat ke kai boothon par EVM kharaab hone kii shikaayat ai he
 The EVM button is not working at booth number 132 of Chainpur
 vahiin, dalatonganj ke booth number 181 or haidernagara ke booth number 101 par iviem kharaab he
 EVM is also bad at Kewus Nizamat booth number 223, 221 of Samastipur seat in Bihar
 iske alaava samastipur ke dhuralakh main booth sankhya 88 par iviem kharaab hone ke kaaran matdaan baadhit he
 There is a long line at the polling station and voters are creating a ruckus
 samastipur ke bhagirathpur panchayat main 7 hajaar se adhik matadaataaon ne matdaan kaa bahishkaar kiya he
 Workers will not vote due to the closure of the jute mill for two years
 pashchim bengal ke bardwan purv ke bhediya hai skool or galasi ke bahir ghanya main booth number 267 par iviem mashin kharaab hone ke kaaran voting shuru nahin ho pai
 There are also complaints of EVM malfunction from Birbhum
 veerbhum main to updravi iviem lekar hi bhaag gaye
 Bengal has the highest number of reported violence in elections
 uttar pradesh ke kannauj main bhi iviem kharaab hone kii shikaayat he

 sapa kaa aarope he ki kannauj loksabhaa kii chhibramau vidhansabha main booth sankhya- 189 main teen baar iviem badalane ke baad bhi abhi tak matdaan baadhit he

 samaajawaadee party ne chunaav ayog se isaki shikaayat bhi kii he

 agar plane kii betry khatm hone se pehle blike box nahin mila to accident kii vajah kaa pataa laga paanaa naammumkin hoga
 The search operation has been stopped due to bad weather

 By law, the black box should send such signals so that its status can be known at least 30 days after an accident
 agar blike box nahin mila to accident ke kaarnon kaa pataa laga paanaa naammumkin hoga

 yah upkaran 30 inch lanbaa belan kii aakaar kaa microphone he jise ek pot ke madhyam se pani main daalkar sanket pakadaney kaa prayaas kiya jaataa he
 This device can catch black box signals from an average distance of one mile
 baharhaal blike box kii betry samaapt hone tak yah uske sanket nahin hasil kiye gaye to jaanch main juty team said scan sonar naam ke ek upkaran kaa istemaal karenge jo mahaasaagar kii sataha kaa eksre kar saktaa he
 This may allow experts to detect an unusual object in the ocean surface that is not connected to the ocean
 kharaab mausam ne roka khoji abhiyanmalaysia ke laapata vimaan kii khoj se jude abhiyaan ko kharaab mausam kii vajah se roak diya gaya he

 shahar ke bahari hisse main brigade archards main vishwa stareey sports arena ke udghaatan ke liye yahaan aae wa ne kaha ki rahane ne khud ko mahaan ballebaaj sachin tendulkar ke aadhaar par dhaala he
 Waugh said in the interview, 'I like Rahane and he is a quality player
 vah mujhe kuch had tak tendulkar kii yaad dilaataa he

 uski takanic kaaphi majboot he, vah maidan par chaaron taraf shot khel saktaa he or dharyavan he

 ' When asked about Virat Kohli's captaincy, Waugh said that this Delhi batsman is on the right track as a captain

 isliye nishchit taur par vah sahi raah par he

" bhartiya team main spin ke kaaphi achche khilaadi hai or bharat main jeet darj karnaa kaaphi mushkil he

 wa ne intervyuu main kaha, 'mujhe rahane pasand he or vah stareey khilaadi he

 uski back swing kaaphi adhik nahin he
